#more_bloodlines.1 - Mormont Snowbear
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.1
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.1"
	picture = "GFX_snowbear"
	
	min_age = 16
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_mormont
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = snowbear
			}
		}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = greenseer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			trait = greensight
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = mystic
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			trait = hunter
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = brownbear
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.1" #get snowbear
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = craven
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
		}
		
		prestige = 15
		
		add_trait = snowbear

		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.1" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
				}	
			}	
			FROM = {			
				random = {
					chance = 50

					add_trait = craven
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event ={
						id = 38257 #Notify
					}
				}
				}
			}	
		}
		
	}
}

#more_bloodlines.3 - Blackwoods get Crow
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.3
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.3"
	picture = "GFX_crow"
	
	min_age = 12
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_blackwood
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = crow
			}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = greenseer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			trait = greensight
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = mystic
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			trait = hunter
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			trait = falconer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.3" #get crow
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
		}
		
		prestige = 15
		
		add_trait = crow

		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.3" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
				}	
			}	
			FROM = {			
				random = {
					chance = 50

					add_trait = craven
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event ={
						id = 38257 #Notify
					}
				}
				}
			}	
		}
		
	}

#more_bloodlines.4 - First Man gets Greensight
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.4
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.4"
	picture = "GFX_green_dream"
	
	min_age = 12
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_greensight
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = greensight
			}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			trait = mystic
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			trait = crippled
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.4" #get greensight
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = crippled #I want to fly
			}
		}
		
		prestige = 15
		
		add_trait = greensight

		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.4" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { trait = stressed }
					NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
				}	
			}	
			FROM = {			
				random = {
					chance = 50

					add_trait = stressed
				}
			}	
		}
		
	}
}

#more_bloodlines.5 - Hunting!!
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.5
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.5"
	picture = "GFX_evt_hunting_scene"
	
	min_age = 16
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
		any_owned_bloodline = {
			has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_hunter
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = hunter
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_strong_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = slothful
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = shy
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_weak_trigger = yes
		}			
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.5" #become hunter
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = gregarious
			}
		}
		
		prestige = 15
		
		add_trait = hunter

		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.5" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
				}	
			}	
			FROM = {			
				random = {
					chance = 50

					add_trait = craven
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event ={
						id = 38257 #Notify
					}
				}
				}
			}	
		}
		
	}
}

#more_bloodlines.6 - Mystical gets mystic
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.6
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.6"
	picture = "GFX_green_dream"
	
	min_age = 12
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_mystic
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = mystic
			}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = greenseer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			trait = greensight
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			trait = crippled
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_smart_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_genius_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.6" #get mystic
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2

				factor = 3
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes

			}

			}

				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = crippled #I want to fly

		prestige = 15
		
		add_trait = mystic

		
	}

				factor = 3

#more_bloodlines.7 - cruel gets cruel
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.7
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.7"
	picture = "GFX_burn_alive"
	
	min_age = 12
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_cruel
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = kind
				trait = cruel
			}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			trait = familyperson
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = honorable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = lunatic
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 25
			trait = possessed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 25
			trait = impaler
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = drunkard
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.7" #get cruel

#more_bloodlines.8 - Falconer
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.8
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.8"
	picture = "GFX_evt_hunting_scene"
	
	min_age = 16
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
		any_owned_bloodline = {
			has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_falconer
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = falconer
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			trait = hunter
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_strong_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = slothful
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = shy
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_weak_trigger = yes
		}			
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.8" #become hunter
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = gregarious
			}
		}
		
		prestige = 15
		
		add_trait = falconer

		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.8" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
				}	
			}	
			FROM = {			
				random = {
					chance = 50

					add_trait = craven
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event ={
						id = 38257 #Notify
					}
				}
				}
			}	
		}
		
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_fair
			}
			NOT = {
				character = 77120
			}
			NOT = {
				character = 77014
			}
			NOT = {
				character = 77023
			}
			NOR = {
				trait = fair_2
				is_ugly_trigger = yes
				has_character_flag = flag_secret_bastard
				has_character_flag = mb_fair_check
			}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.13" #get fair
		prestige = 15
		set_character_flag = mb_fair_check
		random_list = {
			60 = { 
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						trait = fair_1
					}
				}
				add_trait = fair 
			}
			25 = { 
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						trait = fair_1
					}
				}
				add_trait = fair_1 
			}
			15 = { 
				add_trait = fair_2 
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.19"
	
	min_age = 8
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
		any_owned_bloodline = {
			has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_tall
		}
		NOR = {
			trait = tall_2
			is_short_trigger = yes
			has_character_flag = flag_secret_bastard
			has_character_flag = mb_tall_check
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.19" #get tall
		prestige = 15
		set_character_flag = mb_tall_check
		random_list = {
			60 = { 
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						trait = tall_1
					}
				}
				add_trait = tall 
			}
			25 = { 
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						trait = tall_1
					}
				}
				add_trait = tall_1 
			}
			15 = { 
				add_trait = tall_2 
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {

			}

			}
		}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = greenseer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			trait = greensight
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = mystic
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			trait = hunter
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			trait = falconer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.25" #get crane
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = craven
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
		}
		
		prestige = 15
		
		add_trait = crane

		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.25" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
				}	
			}	
			FROM = {			
				random = {
					chance = 50

					add_trait = craven
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event ={
						id = 38257 #Notify
					}
				}
				}
			}	
		}
		
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.29"
	
	min_age = 8
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_karstark
			}
			NOT = {
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.29" #get brawny
		prestige = 15
		add_trait = robust		
	}
}

#more_bloodlines.32 - Lothston Bat
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.32
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.32"
	
	min_age = 16
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_batl
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = bat
			}
		}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = greenseer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			trait = greensight
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = mystic
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			trait = hunter
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			trait = falconer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.32" #get bat
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = craven
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
		}
		
		prestige = 15
		
		add_trait = bat

		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.32" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = craven
			}
		}		
	}
}
#more_bloodlines.33 - Lothston gets cannibal
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.33
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.33"
	picture = "GFX_burn_alive"
	
	min_age = 12
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_cannibal
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = kind
				trait = cannibal_trait
		}
}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			trait = familyperson
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = honorable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = lunatic
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 25
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 25
			trait = impaler
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 35
			trait = possessed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 15
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = drunkard
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.33" #get cruel
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cruel
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				trait = possessed
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				trait = lunatic
			}
		}
		
		prestige = -5
		
		add_trait = cannibal_trait

		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.33" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = honorable
			}
		}
		
				random = {
					chance = 25
					add_trait = kind
				}
		
	}
}
#more_bloodlines.34 - Lothston Great Bat
character_event = {

	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.34"
	
	min_age = 16
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		}

		modifier = {

		}
	}

				factor = 2

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.33
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous

			modifier = {

				factor = 3

#more_bloodlines.43 - Great Warg created
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.43
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.43"
	picture = "GFX_skinchanger"
	
	min_age = 12
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
		NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
		calc_true_if = {
				amount = 3
				trait = crow
				trait = wolf
				trait = cata
				trait = dog
				trait = goat
				trait = bat
				trait = great_bat
				trait = eagle
				trait = deer
				trait = boar
				trait = brownbear
				trait = snowbear
				trait = sea_lion
				trait = whale
				trait = shadowcat
				trait = crane
				trait = lizardlion
				trait = fox_mbs
				trait = hrakkar
				trait = lion
				trait = vulture
				trait = direwolf
				trait = mammoth
				trait = unicorn_MBS
				trait = walrus
			}
			NOT = {
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_great_warg
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_winged_wolf
				}
			}
	}
	

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.43" #get bloodline
		
		
		create_bloodline = {
			type = great_warg
		}
	
	add_trait = mystic	
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.43" #get bloodline+nickname
		
		
		create_bloodline = {
			type = great_warg
		}
		random_list = {
			100 = { give_nickname = nick_greatwarg	 }
			100 = { give_nickname = nick_beasttamer	 }
			100 = { give_nickname = nick_manyskinned	 }
			100 = { give_nickname = nick_king_of_the_woods	 }
		}
		add_trait = mystic	
	}
}

#more_bloodlines.52 - Finds a baby in the woods
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.52
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.52"
	picture = "GFX_evt_birth"
	
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.52" #go with her
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = honorable
			}
		}
		location = {
			ROOT = {
				create_character = {
					age = 0
					dynasty = ROOT
					culture = PREV
					religion = ROOT
				}
				new_character = {	
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { is_female = no } }
						set_father = ROOT
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { is_female = yes } }
						set_mother = ROOT
					}					
					set_character_flag = bear_blood_first_generation
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = bear_child
						duration = -1
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						random = {
							chance = 10
							add_trait = genius
							remove_trait = quick
							remove_trait = quick_1
							remove_trait = slow
							remove_trait = slow_1
							remove_trait = imbecile
							remove_trait = imbecile_1
						}
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { trait = genius } }
							random = {
								chance = 25
								add_trait = quick
								remove_trait = slow
								remove_trait = slow_1
								remove_trait = imbecile
								remove_trait = imbecile_1
							}
						}	
						random = {
							chance = 50
							add_trait = strong
							remove_trait = weak
							remove_trait = weak_1
							remove_trait = weak_2
						}
						random = {
							chance = 25
							add_trait = tall
							remove_trait = dwarf
							remove_trait = dwarf_1
							remove_trait = dwarf_2
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.52" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cruel
			}
		}		

		add_trait = cruel
	}
}
# Child getting older, court rumors of real mother being a bear
narrative_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.53
	title = EVTTITLEmore_bloodlines.53
	desc = EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.53
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_narrative_frame_war

	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 13
	has_character_flag = bear_blood_first_generation
	capable_only = yes	
	
	trigger = {
		age = 13
		OR = {
			ai = no
			father = { ai = no }
			mother = { ai = no }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = bear_spawn_rumors }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.53
		set_character_flag = bear_spawn_rumors
		hidden_tooltip = {
			father = { narrative_event = { id = more_bloodlines.54 } }
			mother = { narrative_event = { id = more_bloodlines.54 } }
		}
		prestige = 20
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = wroth } 
				NOT = { trait = patient }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 30
				add_trait = wroth
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38254 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { trait = proud } 
				NOT = { trait = humble }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 30
				add_trait = proud
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 38261 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = humble }
			remove_trait = humble
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.53
		set_character_flag = bear_spawn_rumors
		hidden_tooltip = {
			father = { narrative_event = { id = more_bloodlines.54 } }
			mother = { narrative_event = { id = more_bloodlines.54 } }
		}
		prestige = 10
	}
}

			100 = { add_trait = brownbear }
		}

		
	}

				trait = zealous
			}

				factor = 0.33
				is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				NOT = { is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes }
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					NOT = { personality_traits = 6 }
				}	
			}	
			FROM = {			
				random = {
					chance = 50

					add_trait = craven
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event ={
						id = 38257 #Notify
					}
				}
				}
			}	
		}
		
	}
}

					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_winged_wolf
				}
			}

				AND = {
					character = 8059
					trait = direwolf
					trait = crippled
			}
	}
	

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.60" #get greensight

		add_trait = greensight
		add_trait = greenseer
		add_trait = mystic
		create_bloodline = {
			type = winged_wolf
		}

		
	}
}

#Cat uncovers plot
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.61
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.61"
	picture = "GFX_dark_corridor"
	
	min_age = 14

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		trait = cata
		OR = {
			any_unknown_plotter = { 
				plot_target_char = { always = yes }
				NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
				NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
			}
			any_spouse = {
				any_unknown_plotter = {
					plot_target_char = { always = yes }
					NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
					NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
			}
			any_close_relative = {
				OR = {
					dynasty = ROOT
					is_child_of = ROOT
					is_grandchild_of = ROOT
					is_parent_of = ROOT
					is_grandparent_of = ROOT
					sibling = ROOT							
				}
				any_unknown_plotter = {
					plot_target_char = { always = yes }
					NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
					NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	

	immediate = {	
		clear_event_target = cat_plotter_reveal
		#find plot to reveal
		random_unknown_plotter = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = { always = yes }
				NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner } 
				NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
			}
			save_event_target_as = cat_plotter_reveal
			break = yes
		}
		random_close_relative = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					dynasty = ROOT
					is_child_of = ROOT
					is_grandchild_of = ROOT
					is_parent_of = ROOT
					is_grandparent_of = ROOT
					sibling = ROOT							
				}
				any_unknown_plotter = {
					plot_target_char = { always = yes }
					NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
					NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
			}
			random_unknown_plotter = {
				limit = { 
					plot_target_char = { always = yes }
					NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner } 
					NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				save_event_target_as = cat_plotter_reveal
				break = yes
			}
		}
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				any_unknown_plotter = {
					plot_target_char = { always = yes }
					NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
					NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
			}
			random_unknown_plotter = {
				limit = { 
					plot_target_char = { always = yes }
					NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner } 
					NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				save_event_target_as = cat_plotter_reveal
				break = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.61" 
		event_target:cat_plotter_reveal = {
			show_portrait = yes
			plot_target_char = { show_portrait = yes }

		}

#more_bloodlines.80 - Becomes Greenseer
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.80
	hide_window = yes
	
	min_age = 12
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
		OR = { 
			trait = crow
			trait = wolf
			trait = cata
			trait = dog
			trait = goat
			trait = bat
			trait = great_bat
			trait = eagle
			trait = deer
			trait = boar
			trait = brownbear
			trait = snowbear
			trait = sea_lion
			trait = whale
			trait = shadowcat
			trait = crane
			trait = lizardlion
			trait = hrakkar
			trait = lion
			trait = vulture
			trait = walrus
			trait = fox_mbs
			trait = mammoth
			trait = unicorn_MBS
			trait = direwolf
			trait = greensight 
		}	
		NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_mbs_not_greenseer }
		NOT = { trait = greenseer }
	}
	

	immediate = {	
		random_list = {
			989 = { 
				set_character_flag = flag_mbs_not_greenseer
			}
			10 = { 
				add_trait = mystic	
				add_trait = greensight	
				character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.82 }
				set_character_flag = flag_mbs_not_greenseer
			}
			1 = { 
				create_bloodline = {
					type = greenseer_bloodline
				}
				add_trait = mystic	
				add_trait = greensight	
				add_trait = greenseer	
				trait = crow
				character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.81 }
				change_learning = 6
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}

}

		d_cotf_mbs = { grant_title = PREV }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				}	
			}	
			random_list = {
				100 = { religion = wildling_religion }
				100 = { religion = old_gods }
			}
			character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.99 days = 1 }
			piety = 15
		}
		create_character = {
			age = 247
			dynasty = none
			trait = mystic
			trait = cotf
			religion = beyond_wall_old_gods
			culture = children_forest
		}
		create_character = {
			age = 213
			dynasty = none
			trait = mystic
			trait = cotf
			religion = beyond_wall_old_gods
			culture = children_forest
		}
		create_character = {
			age = 986
			dynasty = none
			trait = mystic
			trait = cotf
			religion = beyond_wall_old_gods
			culture = children_forest
		}
		create_character = {
			age = 103
			dynasty = none
			trait = mystic
			trait = cotf
			religion = beyond_wall_old_gods
			culture = children_forest
		}
	}	

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

		add_trait = cotf
		add_trait = greenseer_weirwood
	}
}

	hide_window = yes

		is_ruler = yes
		trait = nightswatch
	}
	
	immediate = {	
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = nightswatch
			}
			any_courtier = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						prisoner = no
						NOT = { culture_group = free_folk }
						NOT = {
							trait = nightswatch
						}
						NOT = {
							trait = wildling
						}
					}
					banish = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.209
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.209"
	picture = "GFX_knighted"
	
	min_age = 12
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
		trait = master_warrior
		trait = kingsguard
		trait = knight
		NOT = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_kingsguard_forged
			}
		}	
		calc_true_if = {
			amount = 3
			trait = just
			trait = kind
			trait = brave
			trait = diligent
			trait = charitable
			trait = honorable
			trait = honest
			trait = patient
			trait = zealous
			trait = authoritative
		}
		NOT = { trait = cruel }
		NOT = { trait = deceitful }
		NOT = { trait = drunkard }
		NOT = { trait = impaler }
		NOT = { trait = greedy }
		NOT = { trait = slothful }
		NOT = { trait = craven }
		NOT = { trait = arbitrary }
		NOT = { trait = ruthless }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable1 }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable2 }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable3 }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable4 }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable5 }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable6 }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable7 }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable8 }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable9 }
		NOT = { trait = dishonorable10 }
	}
	

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.209" #get bloodline
		
		
		create_bloodline = {
			type = honourable_kingsguard_bloodline
		}
	}
}

######################Skinchanger Society

#On initialisation join skinchangers
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.300
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.300"
	picture = "GFX_godswood"	
	min_age = 10
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
 
		trigger = {
			skinchanger_trigger = yes
			NOT = { society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood }	
		}

	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.300" #join skinchangers
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		prestige = 15
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood } }
			leave_society = yes
			join_society = skinchanger_brotherhood		
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				calc_true_if = {
						amount = 3
						trait = crow
						trait = wolf
						trait = cata
						trait = dog
						trait = goat
						trait = bat
						trait = great_bat
						trait = eagle
						trait = deer
						trait = boar
						trait = brownbear
						trait = snowbear
						trait = sea_lion
						trait = whale
						trait = shadowcat
						trait = crane
						trait = lizardlion
						trait = hrakkar
						trait = fox_mbs
						trait = lion
						trait = vulture
						trait = direwolf
						trait = mammoth
					}
				}
			society_rank_up = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = greensight
				NOT = {
					character = 2126	#don't make Jojen instant tier 2
				}
			}
			society_rank_up = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = greenseer
			}
			society_rank_up = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = greenseer_weirwood
			}
			society_rank_up = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.300" #not join skinchangers
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}		
	}
}

#From on_character_ask_to_join_society
character_event = {
    id = more_bloodlines.305
	hide_window = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
    trigger = {
    	FROM = { any_society_member = { society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood } }
    }
    immediate = {
    	FROM = { 
			random_society_member = {
				limit = { 	
					society_rank == 4
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT					
				}
				character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.306 }
				break = yes
			}
			random_society_member = {
				limit = { 	
					society_rank == 3
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT					
				}
				character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.306 }
				break = yes
			}
			leader = { 
				character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.306 }
				break = yes				
			}
			random_society_member = {
				character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.306 }
			}			
		}
    }
}

#Welcome letter
letter_event = {
    id = more_bloodlines.307
    desc = EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.307
    border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion

    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.307" 
		join_society = skinchanger_brotherhood
		hidden_tooltip = { #add more randoms if lack of members
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_society_member = {
							society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood
							count = 20
						}
					}
				}
				random_playable_ruler = {
					limit = { 
						capital_scope = { region = world_beyond_the_wall } 
						NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
						NOT = { culture_group = winter_group }
					}
					create_random_priest = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = none
						female = no
						culture = THIS
						religion = THIS
						historical = yes
					}
					new_character = {
						change_learning = 2
						random_list = {
							32 = { add_trait = dog }
							32 = { add_trait = wolf }
							32 = { add_trait = crow }
							32 = { add_trait = boar }
							4 = { add_trait = greensight	}
						}
						join_society = skinchanger_brotherhood
						society_rank_up = 1
					}
				}
				random_playable_ruler = {
					limit = { 
						capital_scope = { region = world_beyond_the_wall } 
						NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
						NOT = { culture_group = winter_group }
					}
					create_random_priest = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = none
						female = no
						culture = THIS
						religion = THIS
						historical = yes
					}
					new_character = {
						change_learning = 2
						random_list = {
							32 = { add_trait = dog }
							32 = { add_trait = wolf }
							32 = { add_trait = crow }
							32 = { add_trait = boar }
							4 = { add_trait = greensight	}
						}
						join_society = skinchanger_brotherhood
						society_rank_up = 1
					}
				}
				random_playable_ruler = {
					limit = { 
						capital_scope = { region = world_beyond_the_wall } 
						NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
						NOT = { culture_group = winter_group }
					}
					create_random_priest = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = none
						female = no
						culture = THIS
						religion = THIS
						historical = yes
					}
					new_character = {
						change_learning = 2
						random_list = {
							32 = { add_trait = dog }
							32 = { add_trait = wolf }
							32 = { add_trait = crow }
							32 = { add_trait = boar }
							4 = { add_trait = greensight	}
						}
						join_society = skinchanger_brotherhood
						society_rank_up = 1
					}
				}
				random_playable_ruler = {
					limit = { 
						capital_scope = { region = world_beyond_the_wall } 
						NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
						NOT = { culture_group = winter_group }
					}
					create_random_priest = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = none
						female = no
						culture = THIS
						religion = THIS
						historical = yes
					}
					new_character = {
						change_learning = 2
						random_list = {
							32 = { add_trait = dog }
							32 = { add_trait = wolf }
							32 = { add_trait = crow }
							32 = { add_trait = boar }
							4 = { add_trait = greensight	}
						}
						join_society = skinchanger_brotherhood
						society_rank_up = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						society = {
							any_society_member = {
								is_society_grandmaster = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_society_member = {
					limit = { society_rank == 4 }
					set_society_grandmaster = yes
					break = yes
				}	
				random_society_member = {
					limit = { society_rank == 3 }
					set_society_grandmaster = yes
					break = yes
				}
				random_society_member = {
					limit = { society_rank == 2 }
					set_society_grandmaster = yes
					break = yes
				}
				random_society_member = {
					set_society_grandmaster = yes
					break = yes
				}
				set_society_grandmaster = yes
			}
		}
    }

#MISSIONS

#Mission tombola
character_event = {
    id = more_bloodlines.308
    hide_window = yes

    is_triggered_only = yes
    
	is_in_society = yes

	trigger = {
		society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood
		has_any_quest = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = quest_cooldown_timer }
		NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
	}

    immediate = {
		#If shortage of nearby elders, create one
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					society = {
						any_society_member = {
							count = 2
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							society_rank >= 3							
						}
					}
				}
				liege = { demesne_size = 1 }
			}
			liege = {
				capital_scope = {
					create_random_priest = {
						random_traits = yes
						dynasty = none
						female = no
						culture = THIS
						religion = THIS
						historical = yes
					}
					new_character = {
						change_learning = 2
						random_list = {
							32 = { add_trait = dog }
							32 = { add_trait = wolf }
							32 = { add_trait = crow }
							32 = { add_trait = boar }
							4 = { add_trait = greensight }
						}
						join_society = skinchanger_brotherhood
						society_rank_up = 2
					}
				}
			}	
		}
		#If no nearby elders like me, AI send gift or inform player
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					society = {
						any_society_member = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
    						is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
							society_rank >= 3						
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = { #AI send gift
				limit = { 
					ai = yes 
					OR = {
						AND = { 
							higher_tier_than = DUKE
							wealth = 80							
						}
						AND = { 
							NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
							is_ruler = yes
							wealth = 40
						}
						AND = { 
							is_ruler = no
							wealth = 20
						}
					}	
				}
				random_society_member = {
					limit = { 	
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = -50 }
						society_rank >= 3
					}
					opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = real_gift multiplier = 3 }
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE } }
						wealth = 80
						ROOT = { wealth = -80 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { 
							ROOT = { 
								NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
								is_ruler = yes
							} 
						}
						wealth = 40
						ROOT = { wealth = -40 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { is_ruler = no } }
						wealth = 20
						ROOT = { wealth = -20 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = { #Advise player
				limit = { ai = no }
				character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.309 }
			}	
		}	
    	#Picks out mission giver
    	random_list = {
    		1 = { #International society member
    			society = {
    				random_society_member = {
    					limit = { 	
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
    						is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
							society_rank >= 3
    					}
    					save_event_target_as = skinchanger_instructor
    				}
    			}
    		}
    		100 = { #Realm society member
    			trigger = {
    				society = {
    					any_society_member = {
    						NOT = { character = ROOT }
    						is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
							same_realm = ROOT
							society_rank >= 3
    					}
    				}
    			}
    			society = {
    				random_society_member = {
    					limit = { 	
    						NOT = { character = ROOT }
    						is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							opinion = { who = ROOT value = -20 }
							same_realm = ROOT
							society_rank >= 3
    					}
    					save_event_target_as = skinchanger_instructor
    				}
    			}
    		}
    	}
		if = {
			limit = { event_target:skinchanger_instructor = { always = yes } }
			#Randomizes mission
			random_list = {
				1 = {
				}
				20 = { #Learn from a elder
					trigger = {
						society_rank == 2
						NOT = { has_character_flag = skinchanger_learnt_from_elder }
					}
					event_target:skinchanger_instructor = { character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.320 } }
				}		
				20 = { #Commune with Old Gods
					trigger = {
						society_rank >= 3
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
						}
						is_ill = no
						NOT = { has_character_modifier = skinchanger_communed_gods }
					}
					event_target:skinchanger_instructor = { character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.340 } }
				}
			}
		}	
		#If AI has been in society for long and doesn't have staff, randomly add it
		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				society_rank == 1
				NOT = { 
					any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = weirwood_staff }
				}
				has_any_quest = no
				society_currency >= 500
				days_in_society > 2250
			}
			random = {
				chance = 66
				add_artifact = weirwood_staff
				set_character_flag = has_weirwood_staff
			}
		}	
    }
}

	id = more_bloodlines.321
	desc = EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.321
	quest_target = ROOT

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #accept
		name = ACCEPT
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPmore_bloodlines.321
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			ROOT = {
				set_quest_target = {
					id = quest_skinchanger_learn_from_elder
					holder = ROOT
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.322 days = 20 random = 10 }
		}	
	}
	option = { #nah thx
		name = DECLINE
		custom_tooltip = { text = decline_quest_tooltip }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = quest_cooldown_timer
				hidden = yes
				days = 1000
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}
#Find elder mentor
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.322
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood
		has_quest = quest_skinchanger_learn_from_elder
	}

	immediate = { 
		clear_event_target = skinchanger_elder_mentor 
		#If shortage of foreign elders, create one
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					society = {
						any_society_member = {
							count = 2
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
							NOR = {
								same_liege = ROOT
								liege = { character = ROOT }
								liege = { same_liege = ROOT }
								is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								is_vassal_or_below = ROOT
							}
							society_rank >= 3
							prisoner = no
							is_incapable = no
							NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }							
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = { 
					capital_scope = { region = world_beyond_the_wall } 
					NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
					NOT = { culture_group = winter_group }
					is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
					NOT = { same_realm = ROOT }
					demesne_size = 1
			}
				create_random_priest = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = none
					female = no
					culture = THIS
					religion = THIS
					historical = yes
				}
				new_character = {
					move_character = PREVPREV
					change_learning = 2
					random_list = {
						32 = { add_trait = dog }
						32 = { add_trait = wolf }
						32 = { add_trait = crow }
						32 = { add_trait = boar }
						4 = { add_trait = greensight	}
					}
					join_society = skinchanger_brotherhood
					society_rank_up = 2
				}
			}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }	
				prisoner = no
				war = no
			}
			society = {
				random_society_member = { #find elder to learn from
					limit = { 	
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
						NOR = {
							same_liege = ROOT
							liege = { character = ROOT }
							liege = { same_liege = ROOT }
							is_liege_or_above = ROOT
							is_vassal_or_below = ROOT
						}
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = -25 }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -25 }
						society_rank >= 3
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						has_any_quest = no
						NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
						NOT = { has_character_modifier = quest_cooldown_timer }
						NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_bad_student } }
					}
					save_event_target_as = skinchanger_elder_mentor
					society = { #find mission giver
						random_society_member = {
							limit = { 	
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								NOT = { character = event_target:skinchanger_elder_mentor }
								is_within_diplo_range = event_target:skinchanger_elder_mentor
								society_rank >= 3
							}
							society_quest_event = { id = more_bloodlines.3221 }
							break = yes
						}
					}
					
				}
			}
		}	
		character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.322 days = 300 } #repeat search
	}
}

#Arrive
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.326
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	
	immediate = { 
		clear_event_target = skinchanger_elder_mentor
		FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = skinchanger_elder_mentor }
		if = { #check can continue with this
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_incapable = yes
					prisoner = yes
					NOT = { society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood }
					NOT = { has_quest = quest_skinchanger_learn_from_elder }
				}
			}
			remove_trait = wikid
			clr_quest = { id = quest_skinchanger_learn_from_elder failure = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
				wealth = 100
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tier = KING }
				wealth = 75
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tier = DUKE }
				wealth = 50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tier = COUNT }
				wealth = 25
			}
			else = {
				wealth = 10
			}
			break = yes
		}	
		if = { #check if elder is still available
			limit = {
				event_target:skinchanger_elder_mentor = {
					OR = {
						is_alive = no
						is_incapable = yes
						prisoner = yes
						NOT = { society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood }
						NOT = { has_quest = quest_skinchanger_teach_beginner }
					}
				}	
			}
			character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.328 }
			break = yes
		}	
		character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.329 days = 14 } #start learning		

	}
}

#Start learning
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.329
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.329"
	picture = GFX_godswood
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.329"
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				is_incapable = yes
				prisoner = yes
				NOT = { society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood }
				NOT = { has_quest = quest_skinchanger_learn_from_elder }
				event_target:skinchanger_elder_mentor = {
					OR = {
						is_incapable = yes
						prisoner = yes
						NOT = { society_member_of = skinchanger_brotherhood }
						NOT = { has_quest = quest_skinchanger_teach_beginner }
						is_alive = no
					}
				}
			}	
		}
		event_target:skinchanger_elder_mentor = { 
			show_portrait = yes
			tooltip = {
				random_list = {
					15 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.3
							ROOT = { trait = diligent }
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.3
							ROOT = { trait = ambitious }
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.6
							ROOT = { trait = greensight }
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.5
							ROOT = { trait = mystic }
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.3
							ROOT = { trait = hunter }
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.5

		trigger = { has_character_flag = skinchanger_commune_magic }
	}

		text = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.343C"
		picture = GFX_godswood
		trigger = { has_character_flag = skinchanger_commune_infiltration }
	}
	
	option = {

			text = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.343A"

		}

		}

			trigger = { has_character_flag = skinchanger_commune_infiltration }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = skinchanger_commune_ferocity
			}
			if = {

					NOT = {

					}
				}
				add_trait = robust
			}

				limit = { 
					NOT = { trait = authoritative }
				}
				add_trait = authoritative
			}

					has_education_martial_trigger = yes
					NOT = { trait = brilliant_strategist }
				}	
				random = {
					chance = 20
					upgrade_education_effect = yes
				}	
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOR = {
						trait = master_warrior
						trait = skilled_warrior
					}
				}	
				add_trait = skilled_warrior
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = skinchanger_commune_magic
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { trait = mystic }
				}
				add_trait = mystic
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_education_diplomacy_trigger = yes
					NOT = { trait = grey_eminence  }
				}	
				random = {
					chance = 20
					upgrade_education_effect = yes
				}	
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = {
						trait = greensight
					}
				}	
				add_trait = greensight
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = {
						is_smart_incl_genius_trigger = yes
					}
				}	
				add_trait = quick
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_character_flag = skinchanger_commune_infiltration
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { trait = mystic }
				}
				add_trait = mystic
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_education_intrigue_trigger = yes
					NOT = { trait = elusive_shadow   }
				}	
				random = {
					chance = 20
					upgrade_education_effect = yes
				}	
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = {
						trait = greensight
					}
				}	
				add_trait = greensight
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = {
						is_smart_incl_genius_trigger = yes
					}
				}	
				add_trait = quick
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					any_unknown_plotter = { 
						plot_target_char = { always = yes }
						NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
						NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					any_spouse = {
						any_unknown_plotter = {
							plot_target_char = { always = yes }
							NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
							NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
						}
					}
					any_close_relative = {
						OR = {
							dynasty = ROOT
							is_child_of = ROOT
							is_grandchild_of = ROOT
							is_parent_of = ROOT
							is_grandparent_of = ROOT
							sibling = ROOT

							plot_target_char = { always = yes }

					}

	}

	id = more_bloodlines.361
	desc = EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.361
	quest_target = ROOT

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #accept
		name = ACCEPT
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPmore_bloodlines.361
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			ROOT = {
				set_quest_target = {
					id = quest_carve_weirwood_staff
					holder = ROOT
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.362 days = 30 random = 15 }
		}	
	}
	option = { #nah thx
		name = DECLINE
		custom_tooltip = { text = decline_quest_tooltip }

		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = quest_cooldown_timer
				hidden = yes
				days = 1000
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

						factor = 1.5

					}

					}
					modifier = {

						learning = 18
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.33

					}

#Great success
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.363
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.363"
	picture = GFX_godswood
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.363"
	
		add_society_currency_major_effect = yes		
		add_artifact = weirwood_staff
		set_character_flag = has_weirwood_staff
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = {
					is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
				}	
			}	
			random_list = {
				100 = { religion = wildling_religion }
				100 = { religion = old_gods }
			}
			character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.99 days = 1 }
			piety = 15
		}
	}
	after = {
		clr_quest = quest_carve_weirwood_staff
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = { #5 year cooldown on this mission
				name = quest_carve_weirwood_staff
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#more_bloodlines.401 - Lose aspect
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.401
	hide_window = yes
	min_age = 6
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
		OR = { 
			trait = father_fos
			trait = mother_fos
			trait = warrior_fos
			trait = crone_fos
			trait = smith_fos
			trait = maiden_fos
			trait = stranger_fos
		}
		NOT = {
			has_knighthood_religion_trigger = yes
		}
	}

		
	immediate = {	
		remove_trait = father_fos
		remove_trait = mother_fos
		remove_trait = warrior_fos
		remove_trait = crone_fos
		remove_trait = smith_fos
		remove_trait = maiden_fos
		remove_trait = stranger_fos
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

				religion = yiti_gods_reformed
			}
		}
	}

		
	immediate = {	
		remove_trait = emperor_yiti
		remove_trait = lionofnight_yiti
		remove_trait = maidenmadeoflight_yiti
		remove_trait = monkeytailedwoman_yiti
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

##############Nightswatch Cloaks

character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.440
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	only_men = yes
	
	trigger = {
		trait = nightswatch
		NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_nw_cloak }
		NOT = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = nw_cloak } }
	}
	
	option = {	
		name = OK
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = nw_cloak } } }
			add_artifact = nw_cloak
		}
		set_character_flag = flag_nw_cloak
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.450
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.450"
	picture = "GFX_crow"
	
	min_age = 12
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
		any_owned_bloodline = {
			has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_blackwood
		}
		trait = mystic
		is_old_gods_religion_trigger = yes
		capital_holding = {
			has_building = ca_raventree_weirwood_1
		}
		NOR = {
			has_character_flag = flag_raventree_quest_failed
			has_character_flag = flag_raventree_quest
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 25
			trait = greensight
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.450" #start quest
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = cynical
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
		
		piety = 15
		
		set_character_flag = flag_raventree_quest

		character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.451 }
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.450" #Nope
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = cynical
			}
		}	
		piety = -15
		
		set_character_flag = flag_raventree_quest_failed
	}
}

	immediate = { 
		#randomly add intel to AI
		if = {
			limit = { ai = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = went_on_foreign_tour
						trait = viking

					has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_greenhand 
				}
			trait = mystic
			capital_holding = {
					has_building = ca_oaken_throne_1
			}
			NOR = {
				has_character_flag = flag_oakenseat_quest_failed
				has_character_flag = flag_oakenseat_quest
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			trait = zealous
		}

			factor = 25
			trait = greensight
		}
	}

			}

				factor = 25
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
		
		piety = 15
		
		set_character_flag = flag_oakenseat_quest

		character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.461 }
		
	}

character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.46001
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.46001"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = "GFX_evt_highgarden" 
	
	
	immediate = { 
		#randomly add intel to AI
		if = {
			limit = { ai = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = went_on_foreign_tour
						trait = viking
						trait = ravager
						trait = seaking
						trait = sea_queen
						AND = {
							trait = ambitious
							OR = {
								is_ruler = yes
								martial = 15
								diplomacy = 15
								wealth = 200
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = oakenseat_adventurer #increases probability of intel
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = oakenseat_intel_blackwood_1 }
					b_raventreehall = { 
						has_building = ca_raventree_weirwood_1
						holder_scope = {
							OR = {
								character = ROOT
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_close_relative = ROOT
								same_realm = ROOT
								AND = {
									ROOT = { has_character_flag = oakenseat_adventurer }
									is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random = {
					chance = 5
					modifier = {
						factor = 2.5
						b_raventreehall = { 
							holder_scope = {
								OR = {
									character = ROOT
									dynasty = ROOT

							}
						}
					}

						factor = 2

					}

						factor = 2

					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = slothful
					}
					set_character_flag = oakenseat_intel_blackwood_1

					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						c_blackgrove = {  
							holder_scope = {
								same_realm = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						has_character_flag = oakenseat_adventurer
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = ambitious
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = content
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = diligent
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = slothful
					}
					set_character_flag = oakenseat_intel_ironrath
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = oakenseat_intel_goldengrove }
					c_goldengrove = { 
						holder_scope = {
							OR = {
								character = ROOT
								dynasty = ROOT
								is_close_relative = ROOT
								same_realm = ROOT
								AND = {
									ROOT = { has_character_flag = ravager }
									is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random = {
					chance = 5
					modifier = {
						factor = 2.5
						c_goldengrove = {   
							holder_scope = {
								OR = {
									character = ROOT
									dynasty = ROOT
									is_close_relative = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						c_goldengrove = {  
							holder_scope = {
								same_realm = ROOT
							}
						}
					}

						has_character_flag = oakenseat_adventurer

						trait = ambitious
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = content
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = diligent
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = slothful
					}
					set_character_flag = oakenseat_intel_goldengrove
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = oakenseat_intel_castle_black }

						holder_scope = {
							OR = {
								character = ROOT
								dynasty = ROOT

					}

						factor = 0.5
						trait = slothful
					}

					c_highheart = {

							OR = {
								character = ROOT

	option = {

				has_character_flag = oakenseat_intel_high_heart

		}
		hidden_tooltip = { c_the_citadel = { holder_scope = { character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.4699 } } } }
		
	}

#################################Barrowton back to the Dustins
long_character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.600
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.600"
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			has_landed_title = e_north
			c_barrowton = { 
				has_holder = yes 
				holder_scope = { 
					dynasty = 68				
					NOT = {
						has_character_flag = flag_keeps_barrowton
					}
					NOT = {
						character = 2068 
					}
				}
			}			
			c_fever = { 
				has_holder = yes 
				holder_scope = { 
					dynasty = 79				
				}
			}			
			year = 8284
		}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.600" # Keep with the Ryswells,
		c_barrowton = { holder_scope = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } } }
		c_barrowton = { 
			holder_scope = {
				set_character_flag = flag_keeps_barrowton
				hidden_tooltip = {
					liege = {
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = PREV
							modifier = pressed_my_claim
							years = 2
						}
					}
				}	
			}
		}
		c_rills = { 
			holder_scope = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						liege = {
							reverse_opinion = {
								who = PREV
								modifier = opinion_grateful
								years = 2
							}
					}
				}	
			}
		}
		c_fever = { 
			holder_scope = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						liege = {
							reverse_opinion = {
								who = PREV
								modifier = opinion_disgruntled
								years = 2
							}
						}
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBmore_bloodlines.600" # Back to Dustins
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
		}
		c_barrowton = { holder_scope = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } } }
		c_fever = { 
			holder_scope = {
				d_barrowlands = {
					usurp_title = { target = PREV }
				}
				c_barrowton = {
					usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = PREV }
				}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						liege = {
							reverse_opinion = {
								who = PREV
								modifier = pressed_my_claim
								years = 2
							}
					}
				}	
			}
		}
		e_north = { 
			holder_scope = {
				c_fever = {
					usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = PREV }
				}	#forces Barrowton to be capital
				character_event = {
					id = more_bloodlines.601
				}			
			}
		}
		c_rills = { 
			holder_scope = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						liege = {
							reverse_opinion = {
								who = PREV
								modifier = opinion_disgruntled
								years = 2
							}
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.601
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.601"
	hide_window = yes
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.601" # Back to Dustins
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
		}
		c_barrowton = { 
			holder_scope = {
				c_fever = {
					usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = PREV }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					liege = {
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = PREV
							modifier = opinion_grateful
							years = 5
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					liege = {
						opinion = {
							who = PREV
							modifier = pressed_my_claim
							years = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		e_north = { 
			holder_scope = {
				hidden_tooltip = {
					c_fever = { remove_claim = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			has_landed_title = e_yi_ti
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_living_god
			}
			NOT = {
				trait = god_emperor_yiti
			}
		}
	

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.635" #get trait
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
		
		piety = 15
		add_trait = god_emperor_yiti

		if = {
			limit = { has_nickname = no }
			random_list = {
				100 = { give_nickname =  nick_the_living_god_emperor_1 }
				100 = { give_nickname =  nick_the_living_god_emperor_2 }
				100 = { give_nickname =  nick_the_living_god_emperor_3 }
				100 = { give_nickname =  nick_the_living_god_emperor_4 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			trait = genius

			trait = genius

					NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner } 
					NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }

				save_event_target_as = spoon_plotter_reveal

					plot_target_char = { always = yes }
					NOT = { has_plot = plot_rescue_prisoner }
					NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }

					NOT = { plot_is_known_by = ROOT }

			}

			show_portrait = yes

		#Find baratheon or somebody that knew robert
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				at_location = ROOT
				OR = {
					dynasty = 317
					has_character_flag = flag_knew_robert
				}
			}
			ROOT = {character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.800 }}
		}
		any_character = {
			limit = {
				at_location = ROOT
				has_character_flag = flag_knew_robert_murder
			}
			character_event = { id = more_bloodlines.804 }
		}
	}
}

#more_bloodlines.830 - paranoid gets paranoid
character_event = {
	id = more_bloodlines.830
	desc = "EVTDESCmore_bloodlines.900"
	
	min_age = 8
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
		
	trigger = {
			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_paranoid
			}
			NOR = {
				trait = paranoid
			}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmore_bloodlines.31" #get paranoid
		add_trait = paranoid		
	}
}
